Finally my last comment is a sad one, I was at Glastonbury Festival, I was woken in the early ours of the morning by the sound of a phone ringing, and someone called out "Oh my god!" . then in the distance I heard another ring tone, then another and another, it was as though there was a dawn chorus of mobile phones, then it came my turn to recieve a call, it was so mad. . . the message on my phone from a friend, just said "Michael Jackson has died!!!" I got up, had a wash and walked down into the main food and merch area behind the Pyramid Stage, there were vendors already selling RIP Michael Jackson T Shirts, with the iron on transfers still warm, before his body had even gone cold, it was so sad, to see these people rushing to make one last dollar from Michael.}
